Shen Bao Medical Weekly

Sanitary Facilities in the Improved Rural Area of Shanghai Suburbs   Xiao Shi 213

Poverty, ignorance, and disunity are the biggest causes of rural bankruptcy. However, poverty can be addressed with various proactive methods, ignorance can be combatted with education, and disunity can be resolved through political organization. But physical weakness and lack of mental energy are far more influential. They prevent the use of brainpower for learning, physical strength for bearing burdens, and spare energy for serving society. Thus, farmers' lack of hygiene and proneness to illness are a major contributor to rural bankruptcy. Here are some key points:

Farmers who are weak and often sick spend a great deal of money on superstition each year. They would even borrow money or pawn their clothes to indulge in their superstitious dreams. When sick, they naturally cannot work, and without work, there is no production. How can farmers who rely on labor for a living withstand prolonged idleness? Add to this the cost of medical treatment, and if misfortune strikes and someone dies, even a middle-class farming family can be ruined. The situation is even worse for the poor. These are just the tangible aspects. The intangible losses are countless. From this, it is clear that the need for hygiene in rural areas is extremely urgent. I will now present a summary of the sanitary facilities in the improved rural area of the Shanghai suburbs, organized by the China Vocational Education Society, for reference by those interested in rural sanitation work.

Training Sanitary Personnel: Rural sanitation in our country is still in its infancy, and there is a severe lack of sanitary personnel. The government, constrained by financial resources, cannot address the sanitation needs of remote areas. Doctors, due to living conditions, are rarely able to penetrate deep into rural areas. The only solution is to provide adequate sanitary training to personnel already working in rural areas to spread sanitary practices. Recognizing this, the area has established a sanitary training class, where all working colleagues in the area and local youth gather for a full day of training each week. Sanitary knowledge, first aid procedures, prevention methods, and basic medicine are thoroughly taught by specialized doctors, with practical exercises included. This continuous and indefinite training will invisibly increase the number of people with sanitary knowledge in the 45-square-mile area by dozens, enabling them to handle sanitation work in the area. This is a cost-effective method for poor management.

Implementing Sanitary Education: The high incidence of disease and the prevalence of superstition among farmers are due to a lack of sanitary knowledge. Medical treatment is a temporary solution, while education is a fundamental remedy. Focusing solely on medical treatment without paying attention to sanitary education is like abandoning the root and chasing the branch. The method of education is to first add sanitary courses to all primary schools in the area, imparting knowledge, correcting habits, checking for deficiencies, treating diseases, and guiding simple treatments. In this way, all primary school students in the area will have some sanitary knowledge. At the same time, opportunities are maximized in public education venues to universally teach daily sanitary matters, especially paying attention to women, as women who understand sanitation can manage household hygiene.

Emphasizing Prevention Work: In urban areas, vaccinations are administered in spring and autumn, and prevention measures are taken against cholera and malaria in summer. Therefore, infectious diseases are less common than in rural areas. The greatest goal of sanitation is to prevent diseases before they occur. Treating them after they have already occurred is like digging a well when already thirsty, the worst of strategies. However, how can prevention work be implemented in remote areas? The high mortality rate among rural residents is not without reason. Seeing this, they have paid special attention to the prevention of infectious diseases over the past year. Satisfactory results have been achieved in the prevention of smallpox and cholera. However, the prevention of malaria is more complex and costly, and there are no adequate methods. This year, the incidence of malaria in the Shanghai-Minhang Road area is particularly severe, with patients accounting for more than 30% of the population. The discovery of malignant malaria is even more dangerous. Faced with this situation, their concerns are even greater. Currently, a location has been designated to implement blood testing and fundamental treatment methods, with efforts primarily focused on mosquito control. From this, the importance of disease prevention can be further understood.

Promoting Public Health: Public places in inland areas not only lack sanitary facilities but also exhibit unsanitary phenomena, which can lead to terrible epidemics. However, rural residents lack sanitary knowledge, and public health is not on their minds. The only way to change customs is through the power of education, while also helping them improve all facilities. For example, open-air pits everywhere are the main breeding grounds for flies, so measures are taken to improve them. Filthy garbage heaps are the source of infectious diseases, so more trash cans are set up. Unclean public water buckets can harm the health of all villagers, so their equipment is improved, and public rules are established to limit usage. In addition, floating coffins in the fields and the rotting corpses of animals along the roads are strictly prohibited. By doing so, rural public health will be generally good. They are currently working hard on these aspects and are establishing public health demonstration areas in appropriate locations within the area as models for various villages, with considerable success, which has been praised by domestic and foreign health experts. I believe that if public health can be managed successfully, it will definitely increase the well-being of the public.

Treating Diseases: Many rural residents are poor and cannot afford to hire doctors or buy medicine. They often have no choice but to seek help from the divine and end up dying untreated. Therefore, treating diseases is still extremely important at present. Currently, there is one clinic and three simple clinics in the area, as well as seven simple pharmacies. Rural residents can seek treatment nearby when they are sick. There is no need for consultation fees, and medicine is provided to the poor. With the help of the Shanghai Suburban Advancement Association's Health Committee, specialized doctors provide guidance on treatment methods and resolve all difficult problems each week, benefiting the public greatly.

When the area began its work last year, it started with medicine, followed by all sanitation work. Subsequently, the promotion of other projects proceeded smoothly without obstacles. The importance of rural sanitation is evident. The facts tell us that rural sanitation is extremely urgent. If efforts can be made in sanitation, it can reduce public illness, increase productive capacity, and strengthen public physique, thereby promoting patriotism. Therefore, rural revitalization and national rejuvenation are directly and indirectly related to sanitation work.

Amidst the Anti-Tuberculosis Voice, Our Understanding of Pulmonary Tuberculosis (Part 2) 214

— Zhong Zhihe

Since the severity of pulmonary tuberculosis is so great, we must make proper plans to prevent it in advance. If we have already been infected, we should find ways to treat it properly so that our nation of the sick will not be destroyed by tuberculosis. Therefore, I will list the prevention and treatment methods as follows, which I believe the readers are eagerly waiting to read.

Prevention

(A) Stopping Spitting: Since sputum is the most important cause of tuberculosis transmission, stopping spitting should be dealt with strictly and urgently. This is because sputum is spat everywhere, and through the flying of dust, it unintentionally enters people's respiratory tracts, leading to tuberculosis infection. The methods to stop spitting are: 1. Penalties: (A) The health administrative authorities should issue penalties prohibiting spitting everywhere. Anyone who violates the sanitary regulations and spits everywhere should be managed by well-trained sanitary police, with fines ranging from 30 cents to half a yuan as a warning. All fines should be allocated to tuberculosis prevention funds. (B) In schools and organizations, those who do not pay attention to hygiene, do not value themselves, and spit everywhere should be fined and ordered to examine their own sputum. They should also be ordered to write tuberculosis prevention slogans and draw tuberculosis prevention pictures. This can give offenders a deep impression of tuberculosis and provide materials for the public. Wouldn't this be a perfect strategy? 2. Rewards: Regardless of whether it is in schools, organizations, or institutions, those who carefully and honestly adhere to not spitting everywhere should be encouraged by the authorities with material rewards or certificates. Starting with elementary schools, developing good habits from childhood will have a greater effect.

(B) Expanding Tuberculosis Prevention Propaganda: 1. Film Propaganda: The development of film has become the cutting edge of modern business. The rapid progress of all industries relies on the power of film to promote, cultivate, and implement success. Tuberculosis prevention work can also use film to give our compatriots a proper understanding. 2. Written Propaganda: United tuberculosis prevention associations, national medical journals, and newspapers should publish tuberculosis prevention articles and illustrations to awaken people's attention. Tuberculosis prevention slogans should be posted in busy streets, public places, trains, trams, and buses. 3. Public Lectures: Invite medical experts to give lectures on tuberculosis issues, or go to organizations, schools, and factories to promote tuberculosis prevention, so that compatriots understand the fearfulness of tuberculosis and can prevent its invasion early. Or organize costumed drama troupes and propaganda teams for round-the-clock lecture teams to enhance propaganda strength. 4. Issue tuberculosis prevention calendars, so that compatriots can read tuberculosis prevention knowledge every day. 5. The government should designate a tuberculosis prevention year to conduct large-scale tuberculosis prevention campaigns, such as holding exhibitions, contacting various hospitals and health agencies, providing free physical examinations, and reducing the cost of X-rays to give compatriots the opportunity to examine themselves. 6. Organize a sputum prevention team, which goes to small vegetable markets and other places every morning to politely and gently tell the public the harm of spitting.

(C) Implementing Sanitary Education: 1. Compile sanitary teaching materials and tuberculosis prevention education materials. 2. The health administrative authorities should consult with the education authorities to add sanitary courses and tuberculosis prevention education in schools. 3. Schools should hold tuberculosis prevention debates or offer awards for essays to arouse students' attention to tuberculosis prevention. 4. Train public health personnel and pay attention to the implementation of tuberculosis prevention work.

(D) Sputum Disposal: 1. Spit sputum into a basin containing disinfectant solution, with a lid on the basin to prevent flies from perching on it and spreading tuberculosis. 2. Spit sputum into cloth or paper and burn it with fire. 3. Cover the mouth and nose with a handkerchief when coughing to avoid spraying sputum on others. 4. For sputum scattered on the ground, the health administrative authorities and the tuberculosis prevention association should bring small signs to paste near the sputum, cover the sputum with lime, and mark it with eye-catching symbols to indicate danger. 5. Set up more sputum collection points in public places to facilitate sputum collection.

(E) Personal Hygiene: (1) Quit all bad habits that are harmful to the body to avoid reducing the body's resistance. 2. Pay attention to cleanliness and hygiene, breathe fresh air outdoors, practice deep breathing, and get plenty of sunlight, because the sun is rich in ultraviolet light, which can enhance the body's resistance and has a bactericidal effect. 3. Consult a specialist doctor for early treatment of any diseases in the mouth or nose that may hinder breathing, because breathing through the mouth is harmful to lung health. 4. Eat more nutritious food, reduce worries, and avoid overwork. 5. Promote separate eating and implement sleeping alone. 6. Do not have contact with patients. If contact is unavoidable, wear a mask. Wash hands with hot water, soap, or disinfectant after contact. 7. Those who work with powder, dust, and dirt should wear a mask. It is best to wear a mask when traveling. 8. Prohibit kissing. 9. Join the tuberculosis prevention association and work together. 10. Ask a doctor to check your health once a year.

The Development of Pathology (Part 1) 215

— Yue Qi

—Medical Stories, No. 15—

On the wall of an Egyptian tomb, there are many figures painted. Among them is a young man with a leg that has become useless. Living in modern times, we can look at that picture and say: the young man in the book suffers from infantile paralysis. We know that a certain part of his spinal cord has been affected to a certain extent; we know this for sure, just as we know for sure that the bundle of wheat held by another person in the painting grew from wheat planted underground. But what did the ancient Egyptians think of that young man? Do you think they, like us, would think of the changes inside his body that were different from ordinary people? They would not think of it; even if they did, they would not be able to find out. Because the monks at that time did not allow researchers to dissect the body after death; all he could do was record the external changes of the body.

Page 16

For a long period of time, pathologists could only categorize various external changes they could observe on the body, and combine similar changes into groups. When they discovered a group of symptoms with no variation or slight succession, they gave it a name. In this way, based on the differences in the phenomena of rashes and accompanying symptoms, Sydenham defined the name "measles" to distinguish it from "scarlet fever." Aretaeus's explanation of diabetes—"the dissolution of flesh, discharged with urine"—also belongs to this method of pathological research. After classifying and naming various common diseases in this way, the causes and consequences of each group of symptoms—the frequency of death—were measured and recorded. When the disease progresses on the surface of the body or attached to the surface of the body—for example, injuries with splints, or dermal tumors, or tonsillitis—information about general tissue changes can be discovered. But what if the disease is hidden inside internal organs? Long after the Renaissance, the prohibition against dissecting the body clearly blocked any deeper examination of the tissues of the human body after death.

Naturally, this situation promoted the rise of personal theories about diseases and research methods. These theories and methods still have a certain desolate interest for us, because they are so similar to today's so-called "healing worship," such as: eclectic healing, massage, drug-free treatment, etc. The clever rules applied to all examples are the same. These methods all belong to deduction—starting with theory, then searching for facts to prove the theory. If they found facts that did not match the theory, they would treat the facts with arrogant contempt—as if the facts did not exist. This situation is not surprising, because pathologists at that time could not perform autopsy examinations, microscopes had not yet been invented, and they did not know bacteriology or physiological chemistry.

Common Knowledge Q&A About Diseases 216

— Cheng Hanzhang

(76) Cholelithiasis (Continued)

Q: What symptoms occur after cholelithiasis develops?

A: When gallstones are present, there may be no symptoms clinically. However, when gallstones enlarge, a mass can be felt outside the abdominal wall. The most common symptom is biliary colic.

Q: What kind of pain is experienced during a biliary colic attack?

A: The onset of biliary colic is sudden: the pain is located in the liver area; it is a piercing or bursting pain. The patient suffers excruciating pain as a result. This is caused by the movement of gallstones within the bile duct stimulating the lining of the excretory duct. Therefore, the larger and sharper the gallstones, the more intense the pain.

Q: How do gallstones move?

A: The driving force behind the movement of gallstones includes contraction of bile duct muscles, bile stasis, abdominal wall tension, intestinal peristalsis, etc. In addition, strenuous physical activity, horse riding, car rides, dancing, overeating, pregnancy, menstruation, anger, and fright can also be triggering factors.

Q: Is there a specific time and location for the onset of biliary colic?

A: Biliary colic usually occurs in the evening or at night. Although the pain is usually in the liver area, it often radiates to the right shoulder, right arm, and right chest.

Q: What other systemic symptoms occur during a biliary colic attack?

A: The body often experiences chills and fever, nausea, vomiting, and cold sweats. The pulse is weak, and sometimes it can even lead to unconsciousness and convulsions.

Q: Are there any abnormalities in the patient's breathing and posture during a biliary colic attack?

A: Breathing is very shallow to avoid pressure on the liver area. The posture is mostly fetal position on the right side with knees bent.

Q: Can anything be detected externally in the area of the gallstones?

A: The gallbladder area is slightly raised and tender to pressure, indicating enlargement of the gallbladder and liver.

Q: Are there any abnormalities in the skin after a biliary colic attack?

A: Within one or two days, the entire skin and mucous membranes become jaundiced; the urine also turns yellowish-brown; the stool, however, becomes grayish-white due to lack of bile.

Q: Can the presence of gallstones be detected by X-rays?

A: Because the components of gallstones are radiopaque, they can be visualized by X-rays, which can also determine the location, size, and number of gallstones.

Q: How long does a biliary colic attack last?

A: From one or two hours to several days; there can be intermittent attacks.

Q: What are the reasons for the resolution of a biliary colic attack?

Q: The resolution of a biliary colic attack is due to the gallstone moving from the bile duct into the intestine, or back into the gallbladder, or settling in the bile duct while the mucous membrane and bile duct muscle contraction cease. It can also be caused by the gallstone falling into a wider bile duct, or the gallstone crumbling. These are all reasons for the resolution of biliary colic.

Common Knowledge of Ear, Nose, Throat, and Eye Hygiene 217

— Tang Renjin

(74) Foreign Bodies in the Trachea and Bronchi

I have already discussed foreign bodies in the ear, nose, and throat separately. Now, the last type of foreign body I will discuss is foreign bodies in the trachea and bronchi, which is the most dangerous of the four types. They can be transformed from foreign bodies in the larynx (see previous issue). However, its biggest cause is really due to a sucking action. When children are playing, they often have objects in their mouths. If they suddenly cry, laugh, or get startled, the object in their mouth can be sucked into the trachea and bronchi along with the inhaled air. Thus, the formation of foreign bodies in the trachea and bronchi relies on a sucking action. This is a very clear fact. When adults have objects in their mouths, it is usually very small. So even if there is a sucking action, no harm will be caused. It is best for children not to have objects in their mouths, and they are more likely to cry and get startled, so objects in their mouths can be sucked into the trachea and bronchi at any time along with inhaled air, resulting in foreign bodies in the trachea and bronchi. Therefore, this disease, according to factual demonstration and clinical reports, occurs most often in children under the age of five.

The types of foreign bodies in the trachea and bronchi most commonly include small bamboo or white iron flutes (commonly known as "jiao jiao"), fruit pits, beans, rice grains, food scraps, chess pieces, and buttons. Metal pieces, bone fragments, and coins are less common.

The main symptoms of foreign bodies in the trachea and bronchi are frequent coughing, which is almost always present. And it often leads to breathing difficulties. If the foreign body is not removed immediately at this time, it can cause dangerous symptoms such as bronchitis, pneumonia, and suffocation. Many people have died as a result. Also worth noting is that after small foreign bodies enter the bronchi, coughing may temporarily stop. People often suspect that there is no foreign body present. But the result still causes symptoms such as bronchitis and pneumonia. In medicine, this type of foreign body is specifically called a chronic foreign body.

The most accurate diagnosis of this disease is to use X-rays for fluoroscopy and photography, or to perform a direct bronchoscopy. Its only treatment method is to first insert a bronchoscope after determining the location of the foreign body, and then use forceps to remove it. If breathing difficulties are obvious, then a tracheotomy should be performed first to save breathing, and then try to remove the foreign body.

Although this disease can be treated with first aid, it is still dangerous. Furthermore, families often do not want surgery, and inland hospitals may not have this special medical equipment. Therefore, the safest and simplest way is to pay attention to prevention. The most important preventative measures are four points:

Infants who have not yet developed teeth should not be given foods with pits or hard foods (especially when they are crying).

Parents should teach children not to put flutes, fruit pits, beans, chess pieces, buttons, metal pieces, and coins in their mouths when playing.

Small bamboo or white iron flutes (commonly known as "jiao jiao") rely entirely on the sucking action of the lips to make sound during play. Therefore, they are most easily sucked into the airway. I hope that parents will not buy them for their children.

Vendors selling this type of flute should be banned.

Common Knowledge Q&A About Teeth (14) 218

— Lin Jianxian

(Question 81) What changes occur on the face when acute symptoms erupt?

(Answer) The side of the face near the affected tooth is generally swollen and raised.

(Question 82) How does an acute symptom resolve?

(Answer) Usually within a week, pus naturally penetrates the alveolar bone and breaks through the gum on the cheek or lip. After the pus is completely drained, all symptoms quickly disappear. Surgical incision or drilling to release the pus can alleviate the symptoms earlier. However, many patients believe that the disease is gone after the swelling and pain subside, and no longer seek medical treatment. As a result, the root cause is not removed, and pus remains dormant, developing into chronic periodontitis. Over the years, when the body is weak and resistance is low, it recurs as acute, cyclically harming health.

(Question 83) What dangers can occur during the acute eruption period?

(Answer) Three dangers can occur: If the disease spreads and pus unfortunately affects the jawbone, cellulitis will occur, which is not easy to treat. If pus accumulates for too long, its toxins are often absorbed by the blood, leading to increased systemic symptoms. If the pus itself enters the blood, it becomes sepsis, with increased fever, weak pulse, vomiting, and a condition similar to collapse, which is very dangerous. When the pus expands and seeks a way out, there is no fixed direction, but it will burst through the weakest point of resistance. Sometimes, it will penetrate the jawbone and break out on the outside of the cheek or chin, leaving permanent scars and ruining the appearance. Or it may spread into important cavities inside the head, such as the maxillary sinus, resulting in maxillary sinusitis, which is also very difficult to treat.

Hitler Insults Chinese People 219

— Li Min

According to a Reuters dispatch on the 16th, German leader Hitler, in his book "Mein Kampf," has a chapter that discusses "Blacks and Chinese" together, which is quite insulting to the Chinese people. Our ambassador to Germany, Mr. Liu, has already held informal talks with the German government. Mr. Fink, the representative of German Propaganda Minister Goebbels, has agreed to revise or remove the chapter in the next edition of the book. Herr Hitler is today's European hero of the illusion of the "Third Reich." Elsewhere, some are "rising with the wind." Heroic fervor is currently permeating the world, and at their feet we catch a glimpse of countless hatreds and resentments. Italy's attack on Abyssinia is precisely to use the blood and flesh of blacks, whom Herr Hitler calls "inferior races," to congeal the throne of fascist heroes. According to Herr Hitler in his book "Mein Kampf," he divides the people of the world into two classes: one class is the so-called "inferior races," such as the Abyssinian blacks, who are currently being attacked by Italy, and the "Chinese," who are also being "befriended" and "assisted" by Japan, all belong to this class. These "inferior races" are naturally "destined for suffering" and should be arbitrarily invaded and slaughtered by the so-called "superior races" on the opposite side. Inferior races are destined to be the victims of those who call themselves superior races. The other class is those who Herr Hitler calls the "superior races." Within this class, there are also distinctions. All white people (except for the Soviet Union) are, although equally ordained superior races with the natural right to exploit inferior races bestowed by "God," there are "most superior races" among these many superior races. Where is this "most superior race" in the world? Hitler says proudly: It is Germany! Thus, Germany is naturally the country composed of the most superior race in the world, and it is divinely entitled to arbitrarily invade, slaughter, and exploit any other nation and country in the world. This is Herr Hitler, who claims to be the great hero of our time, and in his book "Mein Kampf" he has worked hard to express his most correct national view and world view.

Hitler's national view and world view are as described above. Naturally, under this "principle" of his, we, the "miserable" Chinese, are undoubtedly the "most inferior race" in the world today. It is a great honor that Herr Hitler is able to "raise his noble hand" and place us, the most unbearable inferior race in the world, together with the "black slaves" who have always been looked down upon by the "superior white people," which many Chinese people consider an insult. The title of glorious "most superior race" must in fact be seized from the bloody struggle of the entire nation! Then the shameful title of "most inferior race" should also be washed away from the bloody struggle of the entire nation.

Tokyo Morning 220

— Xin Er

The little clock that I bought for one yuan has been my companion for more than a year, and now it has stopped ticking in the lonely room. But this time I forgot the suffering of not having a clock, because every time I wake up early in the morning, when I look at the painted wall of the south-facing morning window, I can clearly tell the time: when the sunlight shines on the pine forest in the painting, where the autumn wind seems to be rustling, it is usually half past six; if there is a bridge or water in the middle, it is already showing golden color, and the golden color also reflects the green leaves outside the window, it is more than seven o'clock, and when it slants further up, it is past eight o'clock.

Although seeing the shadow of the tree in the painting moving, I know that there is some cold wind blowing outside the window, but seeing the golden sunlight, it has the power to make me get up. Here, I also rediscovered the freshness of the morning, which is the most sobering time! After getting up, I first feel a burst of cold, and immediately look at the red glow faintly revealing through the gaps in the jungle, which cannot help but make people feel refreshed. Since I came to this island nation, I have become accustomed to getting up early. After washing my face with cold water, I silently nod to the red light flickering between the gaps in the jungle, and push open the glass door, stepping on the rustling gravel path, and walk along the fence and wooden house boards. The water in the small ditch flows slowly, wrapping the sweet and quiet morning air, red, yellow, half red and half yellow, green leaves, silently accompanying the calm and elegant walls and windows of each house, matching the vast blue clouds in the sky. At this time, I completely forget my frustration, my wandering in a foreign country, and my accumulated sadness. I just listen to the strange and interesting tone of my own wooden clogs stepping on the gravel road, and revel in this quiet place, like a beautiful countryside. Can a wanderer who has been rolling in the turbulent waves for a long time get this moment of rest? Sometimes when I realize myself, I pretend to wake up from a dream and ask myself in surprise!

After stepping on the gravel road, there is already the clanging sound of horses' hooves, this is the horse field, separated by a wide road, and on the other side is the mountain grassland of Takadanobaba. I glide across the blue sky again from the still not yet yellow green grass on the mountain, looking at the bright red sun, and my steps are lighter and faster. Climbing the mountain, I often fall down because the dew is still melting, and the ground is wet and slippery, but climbing high on the green grass on the mountain is too refreshing.

Autumn is waning, the weather is still very high and refreshing, and azure morning clouds float in the bright white morning sky. The wind blowing in my face is indeed cold, but I only feel that it makes my head light and refreshed, and I feel that my clothes are cumbersome. At this time, the cold wind becomes something worth thanking. The sunlight awakens the creatures on the ground. Standing on the flower plateau, overlooking the belt of trees beside the train tracks, birds fly up to meet the sun, and although the sound of crows is not wonderful, it always symbolizes an upward mood. Dogs emerge from the forest, followed by people showing their faces. There are also faint sounds of roosters crowing, and listening intently in the tranquility, there is another kind of artistic conception that is not found in the city.

Under the mountain, in front of the earthen cave, by the den with weeds as a door, the homeless wanderers sit quietly, exposing their lonely faces, basking in the sun. I carefully observe and realize that they have already burned a pile of fire in front of them with messy grass, and the ashes still have a slight smoke. At this time, people are turning on the fire basins, and the burrows of these homeless wanderers are even colder!

Looking over to the left, a few low, dilapidated wooden houses appear desolate. A little girl is standing at the door of one of the houses, stretching out a pair of red, frozen, shivering little hands, probably also looking at the sun! It is a pity that the sun is difficult to shine under the mountain, which is blocked by the mountain.

I often revel in this beautiful, calm, fresh, pure morning air, silently watching the whole of Tokyo shrouded in stillness, and forgetting my sadness. However, in quiet times, it is precisely when I am deeply immersed in contemplation, facing the desolate little girl in front of the dilapidated house under the mountain, the homeless wanderer beside the grass burrow, and my own frustrated and haggard shadow, shaking again. This beautiful and clear morning in a foreign country - although it can make me temporarily forget this infinite sadness, it cannot bury it!

Seeking Employment 221

— Ai Tu

That was two years ago. I had just left school not long ago, and I was quietly stranded in Taicheng, not far from my home. At that time, the wind sweeping in from the suburbs and the river was so cold as it blew along the clean and tidy streets. Like many other unemployed young people who had just run out of school, I wore a look of melancholy and anxiety, running around in groups of intellectuals. As usual, the Zuoxin Printing Company became a place where many strangers gathered.

Boss Yu was an optimist. He always bit on his pipe and slowly puffed out gray-white smoke rings, glaring at the students who came in to buy stationery and the women who came out of the countryside. However, he was able to handle the bill collectors and the affairs of the store on the one hand, while very deftly greeting the many young people who had been or had not been teachers, who came and went. His appearance made me feel that he was extremely busy, but in fact, he was very leisurely. Every day, he would always take these guests to the teahouse four or five times to pass the time. This was of course due to his generosity. In fact, in the entire county and township, or rather in the entire county seat, all the school supplies and printed matter were concentrated in his company, and these many young and middle-aged people were his customers.

Strangely enough, I had only just met him then, because I often went to his store to sleep with some friends who were looking for jobs, such as those who hoped to become principals. In this way, I was "treated" by Boss Yu several times. Moreover, I went to his place every day. Besides talking to the boss, I could very clearly see the anxious faces of many people who were much more at a loss than I was. One day, I ran into the Zuoxin Printing Company from the office of a financier who was also a county councilor, carrying a sense of depression and disappointment. Boss Yu smiled and said to me:

"Brother Feng, do you know? Pingzhou has a good chance of becoming the principal of Risheng Elementary School. He's like a brother to you, so you can definitely get a job safely. I congratulate you!"

As he spoke, his drunk-looking red face smiled excitedly, twitching non-stop.

When he said this to me, I immediately picked up the telephone and called Pingzhou:

"What? Remember, you and I have suffered the same hardships!"

However, the words that came from the telephone dealt me a serious blow:

"This is really not easy. You know, even if I become the principal, I don't have the right to hire teachers. Now, the school board appoints them based on the seniority of the family in the genealogy. Each family occupies several teacher positions. In fact, there are currently more than one hundred intellectuals at home who are unemployed, who have returned from Shanghai, Beijing, and Guangzhou, and at the same time, there are a large number of graduates from the county high school and normal school. How can these dozen or so teaching positions be properly distributed? Brother Feng, you have ambition, why would you run back to do this unpromising little teacher! You must work hard, you can have a better future!"

I was stunned. I sighed and hung up the phone. All that was swirling in my head were sad shadows... Where can I go? How can I live without a job? Rural education has rolled into such a dangerous circle.

"It's no wonder," Boss Yu puffed out a puff of smoke, and chuckled lightly. He looked at me and said, "Our clan is the same. They fought for the principal and teacher positions, and everyone became enemies. There are fewer students, but there are too many people who want to be teachers. This world is as difficult to do business in as it is to do business. Our business seems to be pretty good on the surface, but the debts that are owed cannot be collected. For example, if the school has a disturbance and a new principal is replaced, the new principal will not manage it and will not be responsible for the printing fees owed by the old principal. Really..."

The boss sighed and looked at the people sitting there, whom I did not know, and said:

"How is it on your side, Mr. Li? Has the fighting stopped?"

A tall man in a suit sitting opposite me smiled bitterly and said:

"This is the wonder of the world. The teachers who have already started teaching have been expelled for no reason, and they have even fought. In fact, this is a trick for the powerful people in the village to fight each other!"

"Trick!" Boss Yu smiled and looked at me and said, "Brother Feng! Did you hear that? The principal of the county normal school was appointed by order of Commander-in-Chief ××! It's amazing. There are also ten people competing for the principal of the county's third elementary school, including university students, political science students, high school students, and normal school students, but the introducers are all playing tricks. In the end, the one introduced by Commissioner ×× succeeded, but what about the teachers? The principal has almost no power."

My head was dizzy and my hope of finding a job had disappeared without a trace. After wandering in a group of anxious people for a long time, I left Taicheng, left Boss Yu, and set off on my new journey.

Clearing Barren Hills 222

— From Long

The group of people living in the small place called Yu Le Ba specialize in clearing barren hills for others. Aside from bravely using their ox-like brute strength to clear barren hills overgrown with brambles, they seem to have no other life skills or abilities.

These people's homes seem to be unfixed. Sometimes, people hire them to clear land, and then their extremely simple homes move along with them; for every few miles cleared, the home moves forward once, like the nomadic life of ancient times, living by water and grass. Naturally, the children in the family, and some livestock like chickens and dogs, also move forward with them. The older children go with their fathers or brothers to the front as soon as it dawns, carrying tree trunks and dry branches back home to use as firewood for cooking and building houses.

From afar, one sees a hazy, thick black smoke, and tongue-like crimson flames, rising in clusters, soaring straight into the clouds. The raging flames burn and spread among the tangled jungles, making crackling sounds, mixed with the clear, crisp sound of axes and adzes cutting wood. When women and children see this black smoke and hear this sound, they know that their husbands, fathers, or brothers are earning their food and clothing, using their brute strength and resolute courage to clear barren hills for others.

Clearing barren hills is originally an extremely difficult and dangerous thing. Needless to say, the land cleared is remote and barren. Therefore, their daily necessities and food have to be transported from outside in advance. In the barren hills, they often suffer from bloating due to unclean drinking water, unable to get up and work again, quietly ceasing to breathe.

At the same time, there are two things that make people feel even more afraid. One is called miasma, and the other is poisonous snakes. When land clearers encounter these two things, it's as terrifying as encountering a ghost in the pitch-black night, feeling that their life is not far from heaven! However, miasma is not encountered in every barren hill. As for poisonous snakes, there is always the danger of them visiting bare legs. Lai Tou Xiao Er's grandfather and father all died in the mouths of poisonous snakes. Everyone in Yu Le Ba knows this, and clearly understands that clearing barren hills is an extremely dangerous job. However, what other life skills do these people have besides using brute strength and life to earn a living!

One afternoon, the women and children were strolling in front of the simple attap houses, watching clusters of black smoke and crimson flames rising from the forest in front, floating slowly into the sky, turning half of the sky red. Suddenly, a burst of gongs and drums beat urgently, mixed with a clamorous human voice. The sound slipped into their ears, and their hearts couldn't help but pound. They knew in their hearts that they had encountered a dangerous thing again. (This is a habit of the barren hill clearers. When they encounter poisonous snakes in the barren hills, they beat cloth drums and copper gongs urgently, as if beating gongs and drums can resist the attack of poisonous snakes)?

The women in the back, with pounding hearts, ran to the desolate barren forest, squeezed into the crowd, and asked, "Who is it, who has been bitten by a poisonous snake"? Staring with bulging eyes, short disheveled hair fluttering in front of her forehead.

"Lai Tou Xiao Er, and… a total of three people." The voice coming from the crowd was low and sad.

"How is it, is it serious"? Someone asked with great concern.

"Alas, it's so pitiful, three generations all died in the mouths of poisonous snakes!" The women around shook their heads and sighed, watching Lai Tou Xiao Er's mother, like a madwoman, with disheveled hair and tears all over her face, holding Lai Tou Xiao Er's body and crying and shouting!

After the corpse was carried out of the barren hill, this tragedy seemed to dissipate like smoke. The barren hill clearers continued to do their unfinished work. Clusters of thick black smoke and crimson blood flames still rose between the trees, and everywhere there were the sounds of wood burning, and the sound of axes and adzes.

Broadcasting Program

National Studies 223

Feng Mingquan's "Selections from Ancient Prose"

Li Shude (940) 7:30 AM to 8:00 AM

Topic: "Random Notes from Chun Zai Tang"

The poetry topic was "Smoky Vegetables, Falling Flowers Large." My opening line was, "Flowers fall, but spring remains." Xiangxiang deeply appreciated it, saying, "This is similar to 'A general will fly, but also performs a returning wind dance. Fallen, yet still make up half a face.' His future achievements are immeasurable." However, I ended up being abandoned for life, failing my teacher's expectations. How shameful! Xiangxiang entered and exited the positions of general and minister, personally stabilized the southeast. His achievements were unparalleled at the time. He was especially good at physiognomy. Those he recognized and promoted are countless famous ministers and generals. Only I am worthless. My teacher's ability to judge people is clear. In the fourth year of Tongzhi, I was in Nanjing, staying with Mr. Yu. He mentioned the previous line and said, "Thinking about it now, arriving at Pengshan for the first time, the wind leads back to the country. It truly fits the falling flower. However, I have been living in seclusion, writing about my life, already reaching eighty volumes. Although I dare not hope for a famous mountain altar, if a single word of my poor and sorrowful writing is passed down, perhaps one can also say that spring remains." This is meaningless talk, just to make light of it. What is meant is, "Chun Zai Tang." When I see my teacher in the future, I should ask him to write these three words.

Xia Hesheng's "Three Smiles"

Dunben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening: "Missing Home"

The willow silk is like sunlight. The cuckoo’s voice urges heartache. The heart of a traveler is like a knife cutting. What day will I get to go home and see my parents? I remember, I waved goodbye at the South Port. Now, we are in the north and south, each is a different place. The two old people are old and weak. The young brother studies at school. The family's food and clothing all depend on me. Therefore, I carry a bag on my shoulder and travel to other places. Educating children is my way to live. A plain life is hard to bear. The seasonal salary is fifty gold. Living, and doing the monkey king. In the daytime, I sit quietly by the west window to teach. In the evening, I trim the candles and correct the papers, my mind is distraught. Sometimes, the wind and rain are so wet. I, burn wine to dispel sorrow, but my sorrow is full. Sometimes, the moon is bright and the stars are sparse and clean. I, burn incense and tell heaven. I am afraid that my parents are sick and I cannot serve them. I cannot bring them medicine in front of the window. Parents miss their son, their liver and intestines are broken. The son misses his parents, tears are flowing. Parents call their son, but the son is not there. The son calls his parents, even more sad. Parents, my son is away from home making a living. My heart is at home with the old. Suddenly, it is as if I return home and see my parents. I only see, the two old people have white hair like frost. The family reunion is so happy. Joy fills the room, like crazy. My young brother is, holding a textbook and reading in front of the hall. My parents are sitting side by side asking about my life. Neighbors come to visit me. I am, diligently greeting them, very happy. Serving tea, asking about their health, saying, a guest is not too lonely. Suddenly, three knocks at the door wakes me up. It turns out it was a dream. The sun shines on the bamboo pole, shining on the gauze hall.

Movie News

Aftermath of the Robbery, Peach Blossoms Continue Filming 228

"Aftermath of the Robbery, Peach Blossoms" written by Hong Shen, directed by Zhang Shichuan, and starring Hu Die, has been filming for four months. During which, filming was temporarily stopped due to Hu Die's honeymoon. Now Ms. Hu has returned to the studio and is working again. The set is a purely oriental-style mansion garden, which is very sophisticated. The walls and pillars are carved with dragons and phoenixes, which took four weeks and cost more than a thousand yuan to complete. Filming started the other day. In addition to Hu Die, the actors include Sun Min, Xu Xinyuan, etc. The first shot was Sun Min moving into Hu Die's new apartment. There are as many as fourteen large and small suitcases. It is expected that all the scenes on the set will take two weeks to film, and work is continuing day and night.

Talking About the "Song of Triumph" Actors 229

"Song of Triumph" is the latest sound film masterpiece of Yihua, which took Bu Wancang and many other artists more than a year of painstaking efforts to complete.

Yuan Meiyun plays a naive, clever, and charming village girl, and her performance is moving, with outstanding results.

Wang Yin plays a progressive rural youth, with passion erupting like a lion's roar and sadness revealed like a deer's cry.

Wei Heling plays a primary school teacher, calm and steady, with profound expressions.

Wang Guilin and Qin Tong play two different personalities of suffering old men. Every move makes people feel moved and stimulated. At the same time, they express crying, grieving, anger, and indignation.

Li Junpan plays a domineering, treacherous, and sinister local gentry, penetrating to the core, flawless.

Jiang Xiu plays a loyal farmer, his performance has a unique charm, and his results are surprisingly beautiful.

Xu Zhuodai plays a rice shop owner, his funny movements make people laugh, and his humorous dialogues make people burst into laughter.

Guan Hongda plays a rustic farmer, every gesture and footstep fully express his foolishness and honesty.

Sun Zeyi plays a rural youth who has been infected with urban habits, his performance is excellent, and his results are outstanding.

Other such as Liang Masheng's temple priest, Zhou Xuan and Ge Aina's peasant women, all have excellent contributions.

In short, all the actors in "Song of Triumph" are outstanding actors with high reputations, and all have convenient achievements and excellent performances.
